2016-05-11 14:10:29 SELECT
	`ptt`.`id`,
	`ptt`.`person_id`,
	`ptt`.`duration_days`,
	`ptt`.`certification`,
	`ptt`.`award_id`,
	ROUND((spost.score_value - spre.score_value) / spre.score_value * 100) AS `score_percent_change`,
	`p`.`first_name`,
	`p`.`middle_name`,
	`p`.`last_name`,
	`p`.`birthdate`,
	`f`.`facility_name`,
	`f`.`location_id`,
	`pq`.`qualification_phrase` AS `qualification`,
	`pq2`.`qualification_phrase` AS `primary_qualification`,
	`spre`.`score_value` AS `score_pre`,
	`spost`.`score_value` AS `score_post`,
	GROUP_CONCAT(scoreother.score_label) AS `score_other_k`,
	GROUP_CONCAT(scoreother.score_value) AS `score_other_v`,
	`award`.`award_phrase`,
	`budget`.`budget_code_phrase`,
	`viewloc`.`location_phrase`
FROM `person_to_training` AS `ptt`
 INNER JOIN `person` AS `p` ON p.id = ptt.person_id
 LEFT JOIN `facility` AS `f` ON p.facility_id = f.id
 LEFT JOIN `person_qualification_option` AS `pq` ON p.primary_qualification_option_id = pq.id
 LEFT JOIN `person_qualification_option` AS `pq2` ON pq.parent_id = pq2.id
 LEFT JOIN `score` AS `spre` ON spre.person_to_training_id = ptt.id AND spre.score_label = 'Pre-Test'
 LEFT JOIN `score` AS `spost` ON spost.person_to_training_id = ptt.id AND spost.score_label = 'Post-Test'
 LEFT JOIN `score` AS `scoreother` ON scoreother.person_to_training_id = ptt.id AND scoreother.score_label != 'Post-Test' AND scoreother.score_label != 'Pre-Test'
 LEFT JOIN `person_to_training_award_option` AS `award` ON award.id   = award_id
 LEFT JOIN `person_to_training_budget_option` AS `budget` ON budget.id  = budget_code_option_id
 LEFT JOIN `person_to_training_viewing_loc_option` AS `viewloc` ON viewloc.id = viewing_location_option_id
WHERE
	(ptt.training_id = 984 and p.is_deleted=0 )
GROUP BY
	`ptt`.`id`
ORDER BY
	`last_name` ASC

	`spost`.`score_value` AS `score_post`,
	GROUP_CONCAT(scoreother.score_label) AS `score_other_k`,
	GROUP_CONCAT(scoreother.score_value) AS `score_other_v`,

	`viewloc`.`location_phrase`

2016-05-11 16:19:55 SELECT
	`ptt`.`id`,
	`ptt`.`person_id`,
	`ptt`.`duration_days`,
	`ptt`.`certification`,
	`ptt`.`award_id`,
	ROUND((spost.score_value - spre.score_value) / spre.score_value * 100) AS `score_percent_change`,
	`p`.`first_name`,
	`p`.`middle_name`,
	`p`.`last_name`,
	`p`.`birthdate`,
	`f`.`facility_name`,
	`f`.`location_id`,
	`pq`.`qualification_phrase` AS `qualification`,
	`pq2`.`qualification_phrase` AS `primary_qualification`,
	`spre`.`score_value` AS `score_pre`,
	`spost`.`score_value` AS `score_post`,
	GROUP_CONCAT(scoreother.score_label) AS `score_other_k`,
	GROUP_CONCAT(scoreother.score_value) AS `score_other_v`,
	`award`.`award_phrase`,
	`budget`.`budget_code_phrase`,
	`viewloc`.`location_phrase`
FROM `person_to_training` AS `ptt`
 INNER JOIN `person` AS `p` ON p.id = ptt.person_id
 LEFT JOIN `facility` AS `f` ON p.facility_id = f.id
 LEFT JOIN `person_qualification_option` AS `pq` ON p.primary_qualification_option_id = pq.id
 LEFT JOIN `person_qualification_option` AS `pq2` ON pq.parent_id = pq2.id
 LEFT JOIN `score` AS `spre` ON spre.person_to_training_id = ptt.id AND spre.score_label = 'Pre-Test'
 LEFT JOIN `score` AS `spost` ON spost.person_to_training_id = ptt.id AND spost.score_label = 'Post-Test'
 LEFT JOIN `score` AS `scoreother` ON scoreother.person_to_training_id = ptt.id AND scoreother.score_label != 'Post-Test' AND scoreother.score_label != 'Pre-Test'
 LEFT JOIN `person_to_training_award_option` AS `award` ON award.id   = award_id
 LEFT JOIN `person_to_training_budget_option` AS `budget` ON budget.id  = budget_code_option_id
 LEFT JOIN `person_to_training_viewing_loc_option` AS `viewloc` ON viewloc.id = viewing_location_option_id
WHERE
	(ptt.training_id = 989 and p.is_deleted=0 )
GROUP BY
	`ptt`.`id`
ORDER BY
	`last_name` ASC
2016-05-11 16:29:22 SELECT
	`training`.*,
	GROUP_CONCAT(tt.training_topic_phrase ORDER BY training_topic_phrase SEPARATOR ', ') AS `topics`,
	`ptot`.`training_id`,
	`ptot`.`certification`,
	`too`.`training_organizer_phrase`,
	`p`.`id`,
	`t`.`training_title_phrase` AS `training_title`,
	`tc`.`training_location_name`
FROM `training`
 INNER JOIN `person_to_training` AS `ptot` ON training.id = ptot.training_id
 LEFT JOIN `training_organizer_option` AS `too` ON training.training_organizer_option_id = too.id
 INNER JOIN `person` AS `p` ON p.id = ptot.person_id
 INNER JOIN `training_title_option` AS `t` ON training_title_option_id = t.id
 LEFT JOIN `training_to_training_topic_option` AS `ttt` ON ttt.training_id = training.id
 LEFT JOIN `training_topic_option` AS `tt` ON tt.id = ttt.training_topic_option_id
 INNER JOIN `training_location` AS `tc` ON training.training_location_id = tc.id
WHERE
	(p.id = 3718)
	AND (training.is_deleted = 0)
GROUP BY
	`training`.`id`
ORDER BY
	`training_start_date` DESC

	`p`.`last_name`,
	`p`.`birthdate`,
	`f`.`facility_name`,
	`f`.`location_id`,
	`pq`.`qualification_phrase` AS `qualification`,
	`pq2`.`qualification_phrase` AS `primary_qualification`,
	`spre`.`score_value` AS `score_pre`,
	`spost`.`score_value` AS `score_post`,
	GROUP_CONCAT(scoreother.score_label) AS `score_other_k`,
	GROUP_CONCAT(scoreother.score_value) AS `score_other_v`,
	`award`.`award_phrase`,
	`budget`.`budget_code_phrase`,
	`viewloc`.`location_phrase`
FROM `person_to_training` AS `ptt`
 INNER JOIN `person` AS `p` ON p.id = ptt.person_id
 LEFT JOIN `facility` AS `f` ON p.facility_id = f.id
 LEFT JOIN `person_qualification_option` AS `pq` ON p.primary_qualification_option_id = pq.id
 LEFT JOIN `person_qualification_option` AS `pq2` ON pq.parent_id = pq2.id
 LEFT JOIN `score` AS `spre` ON spre.person_to_training_id = ptt.id AND spre.score_label = 'Pre-Test'
 LEFT JOIN `score` AS `spost` ON spost.person_to_training_id = ptt.id AND spost.score_label = 'Post-Test'
 LEFT JOIN `score` AS `scoreother` ON scoreother.person_to_training_id = ptt.id AND scoreother.score_label != 'Post-Test' AND scoreother.score_label != 'Pre-Test'
 LEFT JOIN `person_to_training_award_option` AS `award` ON award.id   = award_id
 LEFT JOIN `person_to_training_budget_option` AS `budget` ON budget.id  = budget_code_option_id
 LEFT JOIN `person_to_training_viewing_loc_option` AS `viewloc` ON viewloc.id = viewing_location_option_id
WHERE
	(ptt.training_id = 991 and p.is_deleted=0 )
GROUP BY
	`ptt`.`id`
ORDER BY
	`last_name` ASC

	`training`.*,
	GROUP_CONCAT(tt.training_topic_phrase ORDER BY training_topic_phrase SEPARATOR ', ') AS `topics`,
	`ptot`.`training_id`,
	`ptot`.`certification`,
	`too`.`training_organizer_phrase`,
	`p`.`id`,
	`t`.`training_title_phrase` AS `training_title`,
	`tc`.`training_location_name`
FROM `training`
 INNER JOIN `person_to_training` AS `ptot` ON training.id = ptot.training_id
 LEFT JOIN `training_organizer_option` AS `too` ON training.training_organizer_option_id = too.id
 INNER JOIN `person` AS `p` ON p.id = ptot.person_id
 INNER JOIN `training_title_option` AS `t` ON training_title_option_id = t.id
 LEFT JOIN `training_to_training_topic_option` AS `ttt` ON ttt.training_id = training.id
 LEFT JOIN `training_topic_option` AS `tt` ON tt.id = ttt.training_topic_option_id
 INNER JOIN `training_location` AS `tc` ON training.training_location_id = tc.id
WHERE
	(p.id = 4559)
	AND (training.is_deleted = 0)
GROUP BY
	`training`.`id`
ORDER BY
	`training_start_date` DESC
